     {/* 成交量 */}
                  <div style={{ height: 60 }}>
                    <div className="text-[9px] text-white/30 px-1">VOL  MA5</div>
                    <ResponsiveContainer width="100%" height="calc(100% - 14px)">
                      <ComposedChart data={chartData} margin={{ top: 0, right: 4, bottom: 0, left: 0 }}>
                        <XAxis dataKey="date" hide />
                        <YAxis tick={{ fontSize: 8, fill: '#94a3b8' }} width={48} tickFormatter={fmtWan} />
                        <Bar dataKey="volume" isAnimationActive={false}>
                          {chartData.map((d, i) => <Cell key={i} fill={d.isUp ? RISE : FALL} opacity={0.75} />)}
                        </Bar>
                        <Line type="monotone" dataKey="vol5avg" stroke="#facc15" dot={false} strokeWidth={1} isAnimationActive={false} />
                      </ComposedChart>
                    </ResponsiveContainer>
                  </div>

                  {/* MACD + SKDJ 并排 */}
                  <div className="flex gap-1">
                    {/* MACD */}
                    <div className="flex-1 min-w-0" style={{ height: 160 }}>
                      <div className="text-[9px] text-white/40 px-1 pb-0.5">
                        MACD(12,26,9)
                        {chartData[chartData.length - 1]?.dif != null && (
                          <> &nbsp;
                            <span style={{ color: '#facc15' }}>DIF:{fmt(chartData[chartData.length-1].dif as number, 3)}</span>&nbsp;
                            <span style={{ color: '#c084fc' }}>DEA:{fmt(chartData[chartData.length-1].dea as number, 3)}</span>
                          </>
                        )}
                      </div>
                      <ResponsiveContainer width="100%" height="calc(100% - 16px)">
                        <ComposedChart data={chartData} margin={{ top: 2, right: 2, bottom: 0, left: 0 }}>
                          <CartesianGrid strokeDasharray="2 2" stroke="rgba(148,163,184,0.1)" />
                          <XAxis dataKey="date" tick={{ fontSize: 7, fill: '#94a3b8' }} interval={tickInterval} />
                          <YAxis tick={{ fontSize: 7, fill: '#94a3b8' }} width={34} />
                          <Tooltip
                            content={({ active, payload }) => {
                              if (!active || !payload?.length) return null;
                              const d = payload[0].payload;
                              return (
                                <div className="bg-[#1a1f2e] border border-white/10 rounded p-1 text-[9px] shadow-xl">
                                  <div style={{ color: '#facc15' }}>DIF {fmt(d.dif, 3)}</div>
                                  <div style={{ color: '#c084fc' }}>DEA {fmt(d.dea, 3)}</div>
                                  <div style={{ color: (d.macd ?? 0) >= 0 ? RISE : FALL }}>MACD {fmt(d.macd, 3)}</div>
                                </div>
                              );
                            }}
                          />
                          <ReferenceLine y={0} stroke="rgba(148,163,184,0.3)" />
                          <Bar dataKey="macd" isAnimationActive={false}>
                            {chartData.map((d, i) => <Cell key={i} fill={(d.macd as number ?? 0) >= 0 ? RISE : FALL} opacity={0.85} />)}
                          </Bar>
                          <Line type="monotone" dataKey="dif" stroke="#facc15" dot={false} strokeWidth={1} isAnimationActive={false} />
                          <Line type="monotone" dataKey="dea" stroke="#c084fc" dot={false} strokeWidth={1} isAnimationActive={false} />
                        </ComposedChart>
                      </ResponsiveContainer>
                    </div>

                    {/* SKDJ */}
                    <div className="flex-1 min-w-0" style={{ height: 160 }}>
                      <div className="text-[9px] text-white/40 px-1 pb-0.5">
                        SKDJ(9,3)
                        {chartData[chartData.length - 1]?.K != null && (
                          <> &nbsp;
                            <span style={{ color: '#facc15' }}>K:{fmt(chartData[chartData.length-1].K as number)}</span>&nbsp;
                            <span style={{ color: '#c084fc' }}>D:{fmt(chartData[chartData.length-1].D as number)}</span>&nbsp;
                            <span style={{ color: '#22d3ee' }}>J:{fmt(chartData[chartData.length-1].J as number)}</span>
                          </>
                        )}
                      </div>
                      <ResponsiveContainer width="100%" height="calc(100% - 16px)">
                        <ComposedChart data={chartData} margin={{ top: 2, right: 2, bottom: 0, left: 0 }}>
                          <CartesianGrid strokeDasharray="2 2" stroke="rgba(148,163,184,0.1)" />
                          <XAxis dataKey="date" tick={{ fontSize: 7, fill: '#94a3b8' }} interval={tickInterval} />
                          <YAxis domain={[0, 100]} tick={{ fontSize: 7, fill: '#94a3b8' }} width={22} />
                          <Tooltip
                            content={({ active, payload }) => {
                              if (!active || !payload?.length) return null;
                              const d = payload[0].payload;
                              return (
                                <div className="bg-[#1a1f2e] border border-white/10 rounded p-1 text-[9px] shadow-xl">
                                  <div style={{ color: '#facc15' }}>K {fmt(d.K)}</div>
                                  <div style={{ color: '#c084fc' }}>D {fmt(d.D)}</div>
                                  <div style={{ color: '#22d3ee' }}>J {fmt(d.J)}</div>
                                </div>
                              );
                            }}
                          />
                          <ReferenceLine y={80} stroke={RISE} strokeDasharray="2 2" strokeOpacity={0.35} />
                          <ReferenceLine y={20} stroke={FALL} strokeDasharray="2 2" strokeOpacity={0.35} />
                          <Line type="monotone" dataKey="K" stroke="#facc15" dot={false} strokeWidth={1} isAnimationActive={false} />
                          <Line type="monotone" dataKey="D" stroke="#c084fc" dot={false} strokeWidth={1} isAnimationActive={false} />
                          <Line type="monotone" dataKey="J" stroke="#22d3ee" dot={false} strokeWidth={1} isAnimationActive={false} />
                        </ComposedChart>
                      </ResponsiveContainer>
                    </div>
                  </div>
                </TabsContent>

                {/* 四量图 */}
                <TabsContent value="vol" className="mt-1">
                  <VolChart4 data={volData} />
                </TabsContent>
              </Tabs>
            )}

            {/* 外部链接 */}
            {isListed && stock.market === 'A股' && (
              <div className="pb-1">
                <a
                  href={`https://xueqiu.com/S/${stock.code.replace('.SZ', '').replace('.SH', '')}`}
                  target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer"
                  className="flex items-center gap-1 text-[10px] text-primary/70 hover:text-primary"
                >
                  <ExternalLink className="h-2.5 w-2.5" />在雪球查看完整行情
                </a>
              </div>
            )}
          </div>
        )}
      </div>
    </div>
  );
}

// ─── 数据整合 ──────────────────────────────────────────
function buildChartData(candles: Candle[]) {
  const closes = candles.map(c => c.close);
  const macdCalc = closes.length >= 26 ? calcMACD(closes) : null;
  const skdjCalc = candles.length >= 9 ? calcSKDJ(candles) : null;

  const mas = MA_PERIODS.map(p => calcMA(closes, p));
  const vol5avg: number[] = candles.map((_, i) => {
    const start = Math.max(0, i - 4);
    return Math.round(candles.slice(start, i + 1).reduce((s, c) => s + c.volume, 0) / (i - start + 1));
  });

  return candles.map((c, i) => {
    const bodyLow = Math.min(c.open, c.close);
    const bodyHigh = Math.max(c.open, c.close);
    const obj: Record<string, number | string | boolean | null> = {
      ...c,
      isUp: c.close >= c.open,
      // 蜡烛图4段堆叠（Y轴必须从0开始：base_from_zero不支持，用domain手动设置）
      s1: c.low,                      // 透明底座
      s2: bodyLow - c.low,            // 下影线
      s3: Math.max(bodyHigh - bodyLow, (maxP - minP) * 0.002), // 实体
      s4: c.high - bodyHigh,          // 上影线
      // 均线
      ...Object.fromEntries(MA_PERIODS.map((p, j) => [`ma${p}`, mas[j][i]])),
      // 成交量5日均
      vol5avg: vol5avg[i],
      // MACD
      dif: macdCalc ? +macdCalc.dif[i].toFixed(3) : null,
      dea: macdCalc ? +macdCalc.dea[i].toFixed(3) : null,
      macd: macdCalc ? +macdCalc.macd[i].toFixed(3) : null,
      // SKDJ
      K: skdjCalc ? +skdjCalc[i].K.toFixed(2) : null,
      D: skdjCalc ? +skdjCalc[i].D.toFixed(2) : null,
      J: skdjCalc ? +skdjCalc[i].J.toFixed(2) : null,
    };
    return obj;
  });
  // helper scope
  function maxP() { return Math.max(...candles.map(c => c.high)); }
  function minP() { return Math.min(...candles.map(c => c.low)); }
}
```
New String: ```
// ─── 图表行类型 ────────────────────────────────────────
interface ChartRow extends Candle {
  isUp: boolean;
  s1: number; s2: number; s3: number; s4: number;
  ma5: number | null; ma10: number | null; ma20: number | null; ma30: number | null; ma60: number | null;
  vol5avg: number;
  dif: number | null; dea: number | null; macd: number | null;
  K: number | null; D: number | null; J: number | null;
}

// ─── 数据整合 ──────────────────────────────────────────
function buildChartData(candles: Candle[]): ChartRow[] {
  const closes = candles.map(c => c.close);
  const macdCalc = closes.length >= 26 ? calcMACD(closes) : null;
  const skdjCalc = candles.length >= 9 ? calcSKDJ(candles) : null;

  const mas = MA_PERIODS.map(p => calcMA(closes, p));
  const vol5avg: number[] = candles.map((_, i) => {
    const start = Math.max(0, i - 4);
    return Math.round(candles.slice(start, i + 1).reduce((s, c) => s + c.volume, 0) / (i - start + 1));
  });

  const allLows = candles.map(c => c.low);
  const allHighs = candles.map(c => c.high);
  const minLow = Math.min(...allLows);
  const maxHigh = Math.max(...allHighs);
  const minBodySize = (maxHigh - minLow) * 0.002;

  return candles.map((c, i) => {
    const bodyLow = Math.min(c.open, c.close);
    const bodyHigh = Math.max(c.open, c.close);
    return {
      ...c,
      isUp: c.close >= c.open,
      s1: c.low,
      s2: bodyLow - c.low,
      s3: Math.max(bodyHigh - bodyLow, minBodySize),
      s4: c.high - bodyHigh,
      ma5: mas[0][i],
      ma10: mas[1][i],
      ma20: mas[2][i],
      ma30: mas[3][i],
      ma60: mas[4][i],
      vol5avg: vol5avg[i],
      dif: macdCalc ? +macdCalc.dif[i].toFixed(3) : null,
      dea: macdCalc ? +macdCalc.dea[i].toFixed(3) : null,
      macd: macdCalc ? +macdCalc.macd[i].toFixed(3) : null,
      K: skdjCalc ? +skdjCalc[i].K.toFixed(2) : null,
      D: skdjCalc ? +skdjCalc[i].D.toFixed(2) : null,
      J: skdjCalc ? +skdjCalc[i].J.toFixed(2) : null,
    } satisfies ChartRow;
  });
}
```

   2.游资资金；
   3.机构资金；
   4.主力资金。
   5.由于个股的情况不尽相同.所以进入的各种资金也不尽相同.红绿分明.直观。
   6.祝股友炒股喜获丰收！免费学习与交流！品尝盈利的喜悦！
 应用技巧：
   股市中就是股民和主力的博弈。我们都是散户股民，所以就要紧跟着主力走，也就是看最下方的第四条，即主力量能是否变红。
   ①买股就买在主力刚刚进的位置上，主力量能，变红就买。
   ②主力量能，变绿我们就撤。
   ③这个四量图有句经典语言“你我跟着主力走，一切财富全都有！”
   ④四量图，四量齐红为最美！
   ⑤强弱钝化线：下行是调整或空头走弱；上行是多头趋势，行至高部而平行前进，是高部钝化，实属趋势强股。钝化线的密旨：高位钝化后，不继续涨就跌；低位、回调或底部钝化后，不跌就涨。
   ⑥咱们是跟着主力走 还是跟着散户走呢？答案是：主力！就是紧跟第四条主力量能！我们要和主力做朋友，和主力同步赚钱！

   114 // ─── 蜡烛图自定义Shape（堆叠Bar上层的实体+影线）──────────────
   115 // eslint-disable-next-line @typescript-eslint/no-explicit-any
   116 function CandleBody(props: any) {
   117   // props来自recharts Bar shape，包含 x, y, width, height, payload
   118   const { x, y, width, height, payload } = props;
   119   if (!payload || width <= 0) return null;
   120   const { open, close } = payload as Candle;
   121   const isUp = close >= open;
   122   const color = isUp ? RISE : FALL;
   123   const barWidth = Math.max(width - 2, 2);
   124   const barX = x + (width - barWidth) / 2;
   125   return (
   126     <rect x={barX} y={y} width={barWidth} height={Math.max(height, 1)} fill={color} />
   127   );
   128 }
   129 
   130 // 影线：从 high 到 low，细线居中
   131 // eslint-disable-next-line @typescript-eslint/no-explicit-any
   132 function CandleWick(props: any) {
   133   const { x, y, width, height, payload } = props;
   134   if (!payload || width <= 0) return null;
   135   const cx = x + width / 2;
   136   const isUp = (payload as Candle).close >= (payload as Candle).open;
   137   const color = isUp ? RISE : FALL;
   138   return (
   139     <line x1={cx} x2={cx} y1={y} y2={y + height} stroke={color} strokeWidth={1.5} />
   140   );
   141 }

    57   let prevK = 50, prevD = 50;
    58   for (let i = 0; i < candles.length; i++) {
    59     const start = Math.max(0, i - nPeriod + 1);
    60     const slice = candles.slice(start, i + 1);
    61     const lowest = Math.min(...slice.map((c) => c.low));
    62     const highest = Math.max(...slice.map((c) => c.high));

    64     const K = (prevK * (mPeriod - 1) + rsv) / mPeriod;
    65     const D = (prevD * (mPeriod - 1) + K) / mPeriod;

    67     result.push({ K, D, J });

function calcVolIndicators(candles: Candle[]) {
  const vol5avg: number[] = [];
  const obv: number[] = [];
  let obvVal = 0;
  for (let i = 0; i < candles.length; i++) {
    const start = Math.max(0, i - 4);
    const avg = candles.slice(start, i + 1).reduce((s, c) => s + c.volume, 0) / (i - start + 1);
    vol5avg.push(avg);
    const sign = candles[i].close >= (i > 0 ? candles[i - 1].close : candles[i].close) ? 1 : -1;
    obvVal += sign * candles[i].volume;
    obv.push(obvVal);
  }
  return candles.map((c, i) => ({
    date: c.date,
    volume: c.volume,
    vol5avg: Math.round(vol5avg[i]),
    volRatio: vol5avg[i] > 0 ? +(c.volume / vol5avg[i]).toFixed(2) : 1,

New String: ```
// ─── 四量图算法（通达信公式移植）──────────────────────────
// 辅助：简单移动均线（不足期返回 null）
function sma(data: number[], period: number): (number | null)[] {
  return data.map((_, i) => {
    if (i < period - 1) return null;
    return data.slice(i - period + 1, i + 1).reduce((a, b) => a + b, 0) / period;
  });
}

// 1. 散户量能：牛线/马线
//    MID = (3*C + L + O + H) / 6
//    牛线 = 加权MA(MID, 权重20..1，共20期) / 210
//    马线 = MA(牛线, 6)
//    红：C > 牛线；绿：C < 马线 || 牛线>=C>=马线 → 即 C <= 牛线（非红即绿简化）
function calcSanhu(candles: Candle[]): (1 | -1)[] {
  const mids = candles.map(c => (3 * c.close + c.low + c.open + c.high) / 6);
  const bulls: (number | null)[] = mids.map((_, i) => {
    if (i < 20) return null;
    let sum = 0;
    for (let k = 0; k < 20; k++) sum += (20 - k) * mids[i - k];
    // REF(MID, 20) 用权重1
    sum += 1 * mids[i - 20];
    return sum / 210;
  });
  const bullArr = bulls.map(v => v ?? 0);
  const horses = sma(bullArr, 6);
  return candles.map((c, i) => {
    const bull = bulls[i];
    const horse = horses[i];
    if (bull == null || horse == null) return -1;
    if (c.close > bull) return 1;
    return -1; // C < 马线 or 中间都算绿（空仓/出逃）
  });
}

// 2. 游资量能：MAX/MIN(MA60, MA120)
function calcYouzi(candles: Candle[]): (1 | -1)[] {
  const closes = candles.map(c => c.close);
  const ma60 = sma(closes, 60);
  const ma120 = sma(closes, 120);
  return candles.map((c, i) => {
    const a = ma60[i], b = ma120[i];
    if (a == null || b == null) return -1;
    const A = Math.max(a, b);
    return c.close >= A ? 1 : -1;
  });
}

// 3. 机构量能：MAX/MIN(MA45, MA90)
function calcJigou(candles: Candle[]): (1 | -1)[] {
  const closes = candles.map(c => c.close);
  const ma45 = sma(closes, 45);
  const ma90 = sma(closes, 90);
  return candles.map((c, i) => {
    const a = ma45[i], b = ma90[i];
    if (a == null || b == null) return -1;
    const E = Math.max(a, b);
    return c.close > E ? 1 : -1;
  });
}

// 4. 主力量能：MAX/MIN(MA30, MA60)
function calcZhuli(candles: Candle[]): (1 | -1)[] {
  const closes = candles.map(c => c.close);
  const ma30 = sma(closes, 30);
  const ma60 = sma(closes, 60);
  return candles.map((c, i) => {
    const a = ma30[i], b = ma60[i];
    if (a == null || b == null) return -1;
    const J = Math.max(a, b);
    return c.close > J ? 1 : -1;
  });
}

// 强弱钝化线：斐波那契MA [5,13,21,34,55,89,144,233]，score=sum-3.8
const FIB_PERIODS = [5, 13, 21, 34, 55, 89, 144, 233];
function calcQiangRuo(candles: Candle[]): (number | null)[] {
  const closes = candles.map(c => c.close);
  const fibMAs = FIB_PERIODS.map(p => sma(closes, p));
  return candles.map((c, i) => {
    // 只要最短MA有值才计算
    if (fibMAs[0][i] == null) return null;
    let score = 0;
    for (let k = 0; k < FIB_PERIODS.length; k++) {
      const ma = fibMAs[k][i];
      if (ma != null && c.close > ma) score++;
    }
    return +(score - 3.8).toFixed(2);
  });
}

interface LiangRow {
  date: string;
  val: 1;        // 柱高始终为1
  isRed: boolean;
  qiangRuo: number | null;
}
interface LiangData {
  sanhu: LiangRow[];
  youzi: LiangRow[];
  jigou: LiangRow[];
  zhuli: LiangRow[];
}

function calc4Liang(candles: Candle[]): LiangData {
  const sh = calcSanhu(candles);
  const yz = calcYouzi(candles);
  const jg = calcJigou(candles);
  const zl = calcZhuli(candles);
  const qr = calcQiangRuo(candles);
  return {
    sanhu: candles.map((c, i) => ({ date: c.date, val: 1, isRed: sh[i] === 1, qiangRuo: qr[i] })),
    youzi: candles.map((c, i) => ({ date: c.date, val: 1, isRed: yz[i] === 1, qiangRuo: qr[i] })),
    jigou: candles.map((c, i) => ({ date: c.date, val: 1, isRed: jg[i] === 1, qiangRuo: qr[i] })),
    zhuli: candles.map((c, i) => ({ date: c.date, val: 1, isRed: zl[i] === 1, qiangRuo: qr[i] })),
  };
}

// ─── 四量图组件 ─────────────────────────────────────────
const LIANG_LABELS = ['① 散户', '② 游资', '③ 机构', '④ 主力'];
const LIANG_KEYS: (keyof LiangData)[] = ['sanhu', 'youzi', 'jigou', 'zhuli'];

function SingleLiangBar({ rows, label, syncId }: { rows: LiangRow[]; label: string; syncId: string }) {
  const tickInterval = Math.floor(rows.length / 5);
  // 当前最后一根的颜色
  const last = rows[rows.length - 1];
  const labelColor = last?.isRed ? RISE : FALL;
  return (
    <div>
      <div className="flex items-center gap-1.5 px-1 mb-0.5">
        <span className="text-[9px]" style={{ color: labelColor }}>{label}</span>
        <span className="text-[8px]" style={{ color: labelColor }}>{last?.isRed ? '▲ 进场' : '▼ 出逃'}</span>
      </div>
      <ResponsiveContainer width="100%" height={42} syncId={syncId}>
        <ComposedChart data={rows} margin={{ top: 0, right: 4, bottom: 0, left: 0 }}>
          <XAxis dataKey="date" hide interval={tickInterval} />
          <YAxis domain={[0, 1]} hide />
          <Tooltip content={() => null} />
          <Bar dataKey="val" isAnimationActive={false} maxBarSize={12}>
            {rows.map((d, i) => (
              <Cell key={i} fill={d.isRed ? RISE : FALL} opacity={0.9} />
            ))}
          </Bar>
        </ComposedChart>
      </ResponsiveContainer>
    </div>
  );
}

function VolChart4({ liangData }: { liangData: LiangData }) {
  const display = liangData.sanhu.slice(-60);
  const tickInterval = Math.floor(display.length / 5);

  // 强弱钝化线数据（从 sanhu 中取，已附带）
  const qrData = display.map(d => ({ date: d.date, qr: d.qiangRuo }));

  // 截取最后60条给各量能
  const sliced: LiangData = {
    sanhu: liangData.sanhu.slice(-60),
    youzi: liangData.youzi.slice(-60),
    jigou: liangData.jigou.slice(-60),
    zhuli: liangData.zhuli.slice(-60),
  };

  // 统计四量齐红的比例
  const lastIdx = display.length - 1;
  const allRed = lastIdx >= 0 && LIANG_KEYS.every(k => sliced[k][lastIdx]?.isRed);

  return (
    <div className="space-y-1">
      {/* 使用说明 */}
      <div className="rounded-lg border border-white/10 bg-white/3 px-3 py-2 text-[9px] text-white/50 leading-relaxed">
        <span className="text-[#facc15] font-medium">📊 四量图说明</span>：
        红色＝资金进场，绿色＝资金出逃。散户→游资→机构→{' '}
        <span className="text-[#ef4444] font-medium">主力（最关键）</span>。
        策略：主力变红买入，主力变绿撤出。
        <span className="text-[#facc15]">「四量齐红为最美！」</span>

          🔥 四量齐红！主力全线进场
        </div>

              ticks={[-4, -2, 0, 2, 4]} />
            <ReferenceLine y={0} stroke="rgba(148,163,184,0.4)" />
            <ReferenceLine y={3} stroke="rgba(239,68,68,0.3)" strokeDasharray="2 2" />

The issue is likely `height: 160` on the container but then `height="calc(100% - 16px)"` on ResponsiveContainer. The calc with percentage might not work properly when the parent div has a fixed pixel height with inline style.\n\nActually looking more carefully - the parent div has `style={{ height: 160 }}` and then `<ResponsiveContainer width="100%" height="calc(100% - 16px)">`. The `calc()` string might not be supported by recharts ResponsiveContainer - it expects a number or percentage string like "100%", not a calc expression.\n\nThe fix: use a fixed pixel height for the ResponsiveContainer instead of calc.\n\nUser also wants the layout changed:\n- K线 (top)\n- MACD (below K线, full width)  \n- SKDJ (below MACD, full width)\n- 四量图 (in its own tab, OR below SKDJ?)\n\nRe-reading: "SKDJ在MACD之下" and "最牛四量应该放在SKDJ之下" - so they want all in one scroll:\nK线 → VOL → MACD → SKDJ → 四量图 (all stacked vertically, no tabs)\n\nActually wait - "最牛四量应该放在SKDJ之下" - the four quantity chart should be below SKDJ.    455     sanhu: liangData.sanhu.slice(-60),
   456     youzi: liangData.youzi.slice(-60),
   457     jigou: liangData.jigou.slice(-60),
   458     zhuli: liangData.zhuli.slice(-60),
   459   };
   460 
   461   // 统计四量齐红的比例
   462   const lastIdx = display.length - 1;
   463   const allRed = lastIdx >= 0 && LIANG_KEYS.every(k => sliced[k][lastIdx]?.isRed);
   464 
   465   return (
   466     <div className="space-y-1">
   467       {/* 使用说明 */}
   468       <div className="rounded-lg border border-white/10 bg-white/3 px-3 py-2 text-[9px] text-white/50 leading-relaxed">
   469         <span className="text-[#facc15] font-medium">📊 四量图说明</span>：
   470         红色＝资金进场，绿色＝资金出逃。散户→游资→机构→{' '}
   471         <span className="text-[#ef4444] font-medium">主力（最关键）</span>。
   472         策略：主力变红买入，主力变绿撤出。
   473         <span className="text-[#facc15]">「四量齐红为最美！」</span>
   474       </div>
   475 
   476       {/* 四量齐红提示 */}
   477       {allRed && (
   478         <div className="text-center text-[9px] font-bold py-1 rounded" style={{ color: RISE, background: 'rgba(239,68,68,0.1)', border: '1px solid rgba(239,68,68,0.3)' }}>
   479           🔥 四量齐红！主力全线进场
   480         </div>
   481       )}
   482 
   483       {/* 强弱钝化线 */}
   484       <div>
   485         <div className="flex items-center gap-1 px-1 mb-0.5">
   486           <span className="text-[9px] text-[#facc15]">强弱钝化线</span>
   487           <span className="text-[8px] text-white/30">（≥0 多头，&lt;0 空头，高位平行=强势钝化）</span>
   488         </div>
   489         <ResponsiveContainer width="100%" height={55}>
   490           <ComposedChart data={qrData} syncId="liang4" margin={{ top: 2, right: 4, bottom: 0, left: 0 }}>
   491             <CartesianGrid strokeDasharray="2 2" stroke="rgba(148,163,184,0.08)" />
   492             <XAxis dataKey="date" tick={{ fontSize: 8, fill: '#94a3b8' }} interval={tickInterval} />
   493             <YAxis domain={[-4.2, 4.2]} tick={{ fontSize: 8, fill: '#94a3b8' }} width={22}
   494               ticks={[-4, -2, 0, 2, 4]} />
   495             <ReferenceLine y={0} stroke="rgba(148,163,184,0.4)" />
   496             <ReferenceLine y={3} stroke="rgba(239,68,68,0.3)" strokeDasharray="2 2" />
   497             <ReferenceLine y={-3} stroke="rgba(34,211,238,0.3)" strokeDasharray="2 2" />
   498             <Tooltip
   499               content={({ active, payload }) => {
   500                 if (!active || !payload?.length) return null;
   501                 const v = payload[0]?.payload?.qr;
   502                 return (
   503                   <div className="bg-[#1a1f2e] border border-white/10 rounded p-1 text-[9px] shadow-xl">
   504                     <span style={{ color: '#facc15' }}>强弱 {v != null ? v : '--'}</span>
   505                   </div>
   506                 );
   507               }}
   508             />
   509             <Line type="monotone" dataKey="qr" stroke="#facc15" dot={false} strokeWidth={1.5}
   510               connectNulls isAnimationActive={false} />
   511           </ComposedChart>
   512         </ResponsiveContainer>
   513       </div>
   514 
   515       {/* 四量柱状（由上至下：散户→游资→机构→主力） */}
   516       {LIANG_KEYS.map((key, i) => (
   517         <SingleLiangBar
   518           key={key}
   519           rows={sliced[key]}
   520           label={LIANG_LABELS[i]}
   521           syncId="liang4"
   522         />
   523       ))}
   524 
   525       {/* X轴（只在最后一排下方显示） */}
   526       <div style={{ height: 18 }}>
   527         <ResponsiveContainer width="100%" height="100%">
   528           <ComposedChart data={sliced.zhuli} syncId="liang4" margin={{ top: 0, right: 4, bottom: 0, left: 0 }}>
   529             <XAxis dataKey="date" tick={{ fontSize: 8, fill: '#94a3b8' }} interval={tickInterval} />
   530           </ComposedChart>
   531         </ResponsiveContainer>
   532       </div>
   533 
   534       {/* 底部格言 */}
   535       <p className="text-center text-[8px] text-white/25 pt-1">
   536         「你我跟着主力走，一切财富全都有！」
   537       </p>
   538     </div>
   539   );
   540 }

   545   s1: number; s2: number; s3: number; s4: number;

    30 // ─── 指标计算 ──────────────────────────────────────────────
    31 function calcEMA(data: number[], period: number): number[] {
    32   const k = 2 / (period + 1);
    33   const ema: number[] = [];
    34   for (let i = 0; i < data.length; i++) {
    35     if (i === 0) { ema.push(data[0]); continue; }
    36     ema.push(data[i] * k + ema[i - 1] * (1 - k));
    37   }
    38   return ema;
    39 }
    40 function calcMA(data: number[], period: number): (number | null)[] {
    41   return data.map((_, i) => {
    42     if (i < period - 1) return null;
    43     return +(data.slice(i - period + 1, i + 1).reduce((a, b) => a + b, 0) / period).toFixed(3);
    44   });
    45 }
    46 function calcMACD(closes: number[]) {
    47   const ema12 = calcEMA(closes, 12);
    48   const ema26 = calcEMA(closes, 26);
    49   const dif = ema12.map((v, i) => v - ema26[i]);
    50   const dea = calcEMA(dif, 9);

# 沪深K线 API

## API 基本信息

| 字段 | 值 |
|------|-----|
| Plugin ID | `ea9ecacf-f5ab-4c56-9ed7-2fadaf6e62cc` |
| API ID | `api-oLpZ74noWmBa` |
| Endpoint | `POST https://app-csctj2dvhmo1-api-oLpZ74noWmBa-gateway.appmiaoda.com/stock/hs/kline` |
| Auth | `platform_managed`（`X-Gateway-Authorization: Bearer ${INTEGRATIONS_API_KEY}`） |
| Content-Type | `application/x-www-form-urlencoded` |
| Third-party domain | `app-csctj2dvhmo1-api-oLpZ74noWmBa-gateway.appmiaoda.com` |
| 计费 | 启用，折扣价 ¥0.13/次，原价 ¥0.20/次 |

---

## 请求参数

| 参数名 | 类型 | 必填 | 默认值 | 说明 |
|--------|------|------|--------|------|
| `code` | string | 是 | — | 品种代码，如 `000001.SZ` |
| `period` | string | 是 | — | K线类型：`1`-1分钟，`5`-5分钟，`15`-15分钟，`30`-30分钟，`60`-60分钟，`101`-日K，`102`-周K，`103`-月K，`104`-季K，`105`-半年K，`106`-年K |
| `fuquan` | string | 是 | — | 复权状态：`0`-不复权，`1`-前复权，`2`-后复权 |
| `pageSize` | string | 否 | `10` | 返回数量 |

---

## 响应字段

**成功响应（code: 200）：**

| 字段路径 | 类型 | 说明 |
|----------|------|------|
| `code` | number | 状态码，200 表示成功 |
| `msg` | string | 状态描述 |
| `taskNo` | string | 本次请求号 |
| `data.code` | string | 品种代码 |
| `data.type` | string | 数据类型，如 `stock` |
| `data.candle[]` | array | K线数组，每项为数值数组 |
| `data.fields[]` | array | candle 中每列的字段名 |

`data.fields` 顺序说明（与 `candle` 数组各元素一一对应）：

| 索引 | 字段名 | 说明 |
|------|--------|------|
| 0 | `tick_at` | 时间戳（Unix） |
| 1 | `open_px` | 开盘价 |
| 2 | `close_px` | 收盘价 |
| 3 | `high_px` | 最高价 |
| 4 | `low_px` | 最低价 |
| 5 | `turnover_volume` | 成交量 |
| 6 | `turnover_value` | 成交额 |
| 7 | `px_change` | 涨跌额 |
| 8 | `px_change_rate` | 涨跌率（%） |

**失败响应：**

| 字段路径 | 类型 | 说明 |
|----------|------|------|
| `code` | number | 非 200 的错误码 |
| `msg` | string | 错误描述 |

---

## 生成期代码（TypeScript）

```typescript
const apiKey = process.env["INTEGRATIONS_API_KEY"]!; // platform_managed，密钥由平台注入

interface KLineData {
  code: string;
  type: string;
  candle: number[][];
  fields: string[];
}

/**
 * 获取沪深股票 K 线数据。
 * @param code - 品种代码，如 000001.SZ
 * @param period - K 线类型，如 101 为日 K
 * @param fuquan - 复权：0-不复权，1-前复权，2-后复权
 * @param pageSize - 返回数量，默认 10
 * @returns K 线数据（candle 数组 + fields 说明）
 */
async function fetchKLine(
  code: string,
  period: string,
  fuquan: "0" | "1" | "2",
  pageSize = "10"
): Promise<KLineData> {
  const response = await fetch(
    "https://app-csctj2dvhmo1-api-oLpZ74noWmBa-gateway.appmiaoda.com/stock/hs/kline",
    {
      method: "POST",
      headers: {
        "Content-Type": "application/x-www-form-urlencoded",
        "X-Gateway-Authorization": `Bearer ${apiKey}`,
      },
      body: new URLSearchParams({ code, period, fuquan, pageSize }).toString(),
    }
  );

  if (!response.ok) throw new Error(`HTTP error: ${response.status}`);

  const json = await response.json();
  if (json.code !== 200) throw new Error(`API error ${json.code}: ${json.msg}`);

  return json.data as KLineData;
}

// 使用示例：查询平安银行日K（前复权）最近10条
const result = await fetchKLine("000001.SZ", "101", "1", "10");
console.log("fields:", result.fields);
console.log("candle:", result.candle);
```

---

## Edge Function 代码

```typescript
// edge-functions/stock-kline.ts
import { serve } from "https://deno.land/std/http/server.ts";

serve(async (req: Request): Promise<Response> => {
  if (req.method !== "POST") {
    return new Response("Method Not Allowed", { status: 405 });
  }

  // --- 解析请求 ---
  let code: string;
  let period: string;
  let fuquan: string;
  let pageSize: string;
  try {
    const body = await req.json();
    code = body.code;
    period = body.period;
    fuquan = body.fuquan;
    if (!code) throw new Error("Missing code");
    if (!period) throw new Error("Missing period");
    if (fuquan === undefined || fuquan === null) throw new Error("Missing fuquan");
    pageSize = body.pageSize ?? "10";
  } catch {
    return new Response(JSON.stringify({ error: "Invalid request body" }), {
      status: 400,
      headers: { "Content-Type": "application/json" },
    });
  }

  // --- 注入平台密钥 ---
  const apiKey = Deno.env.get("INTEGRATIONS_API_KEY");
  if (!apiKey) {
    return new Response(JSON.stringify({ error: "Server configuration error" }), {
      status: 500,
      headers: { "Content-Type": "application/json" },
    });
  }

  // --- 调用上游 ---
  const upstream = await fetch(
    "https://app-csctj2dvhmo1-api-oLpZ74noWmBa-gateway.appmiaoda.com/stock/hs/kline",
    {
      method: "POST",
      headers: {
        "Content-Type": "application/x-www-form-urlencoded",
        "X-Gateway-Authorization": `Bearer ${apiKey}`,
      },
      body: new URLSearchParams({ code, period, fuquan, pageSize }).toString(),
    }
  );

  if (upstream.status === 429 || upstream.status === 402) {
    const errText = await upstream.text();
    return new Response(errText, {
      status: upstream.status,
      headers: { "Content-Type": "application/json" },
    });
  }

  if (!upstream.ok) {
    return new Response(
      JSON.stringify({ error: `Upstream error: ${upstream.status}` }),
      { status: 502, headers: { "Content-Type": "application/json" } }
    );
  }

  const data = await upstream.json();
  return new Response(JSON.stringify(data), {
    status: 200,
    headers: { "Content-Type": "application/json" },
  });
});
```

---

## 前端调用代码

**推荐方式（supabase client 可用时）：**

```typescript
/**
 * 查询沪深 K 线数据。
 * @param code - 品种代码，如 000001.SZ
 * @param period - K 线类型，如 101 日 K
 * @param fuquan - 复权：0/1/2
 * @param pageSize - 返回数量，默认 10
 * @returns K 线数据
 */
async function fetchKLine(
  code: string,
  period: string,
  fuquan: string,
  pageSize = "10"
) {
  const { data, error } = await supabase.functions.invoke("stock-kline", {
    body: { code, period, fuquan, pageSize },
  });
  if (error) throw error;
  if (data.code !== 200) throw new Error(`API 错误 ${data.code}：${data.msg}`);
  return data.data;
}
```

---

## 注意事项

- **密钥安全：** `INTEGRATIONS_API_KEY` 仅在 Edge Function 服务端读取，严禁暴露到前端。
- **错误处理：** 务必处理 429（配额超限）和 402（余额不足）。
- **计费：** 每次调用计费，折扣价 ¥0.13/次。
- **candle 解析：** `candle` 是数值数组，`fields` 字段描述每个索引的含义，按 fields 顺序读取 candle 元素。
- **period 说明：** 分钟K（1/5/15/30/60）为分钟级，101-106 为日/周/月/季/半年/年K。

## 生成期代码（TypeScript）

```typescript
const apiKey = process.env["INTEGRATIONS_API_KEY"]!; // platform_managed，密钥由平台注入

interface MinkItem {
  day: string;
  open: string;
  close: string;
  high: string;
  low: string;
  volume: string;
  ma_price5: number;
  ma_price10: number;
  ma_price30: number;
  ma_volume5: number;
  ma_volume10: number;
  ma_volume30: number;
}

/**
 * 获取沪深股票分钟 K 线数据（含均线指标）。
 * @param code - 股票代码，如 000001.SZ
 * @param period - K 线类型（分钟）：1/5/15/30/60/120，默认 1
 * @param pageSize - 返回数量，默认 10
 * @returns 分钟 K 线列表
 */
async function fetchMink(
  code: string,
  period = "1",
  pageSize = "10"
): Promise<MinkItem[]> {
  const response = await fetch(
    "https://app-csctj2dvhmo1-api-NLZ1o2xd6DE9-gateway.appmiaoda.com/stock/hs/mink",
    {
      method: "POST",
      headers: {
        "Content-Type": "application/x-www-form-urlencoded",
        "X-Gateway-Authorization": `Bearer ${apiKey}`,
      },
      body: new URLSearchParams({ code, period, pageSize }).toString(),
    }
  );

  if (!response.ok) throw new Error(`HTTP error: ${response.status}`);

  const json = await response.json();
  if (json.code !== 200) throw new Error(`API error ${json.code}: ${json.msg}`);

  return json.data.list as MinkItem[];
}

// 使用示例：查询平安银行 1 分钟 K 线最近 10 条
const minkData = await fetchMink("000001.SZ", "1", "10");
for (const item of minkData) {
  console.log(`${item.day} 收=${item.close} MA5=${item.ma_price5}`);
}
```

import { serve } from "https://deno.land/std/http/server.ts";

serve(async (req: Request): Promise<Response> => {

  // --- 解析请求 ---
  let code: string;

  } catch {
    return new Response(JSON.stringify({ error: "Invalid request body" }), {
      status: 400,
      headers: { "Content-Type": "application/json" },
    });
  }

  // --- 注入平台密钥 ---
  const apiKey = Deno.env.get("INTEGRATIONS_API_KEY");
  if (!apiKey) {
    return new Response(JSON.stringify({ error: "Server configuration error" }), {
      status: 500,
      headers: { "Content-Type": "application/json" },
    });
  }

  // --- 调用上游 ---
  const upstream = await fetch(
    "https://app-csctj2dvhmo1-api-NLZ1o2xd6DE9-gateway.appmiaoda.com/stock/hs/mink",
    {
      method: "POST",
      headers: {
        "Content-Type": "application/x-www-form-urlencoded",
        "X-Gateway-Authorization": `Bearer ${apiKey}`,

      JSON.stringify({ error: `Upstream error: ${upstream.status}` }),
      { status: 502, headers: { "Content-Type": "application/json" } }
    );

```typescript
/**
 * 查询沪深分钟 K 线（含均线）。
 * @param code - 股票代码，如 000001.SZ
 * @param period - K 线类型（分钟），默认 1
 * @param pageSize - 返回数量，默认 10
 * @returns 分钟 K 线列表
 */
async function fetchMink(code: string, period = "1", pageSize = "10") {

    body: { code, period, pageSize },
  });
  if (error) throw error;
  if (data.code !== 200) throw new Error(`API 错误 ${data.code}：${data.msg}`);
  return data.data.list;

## 注意事项

- **密钥安全：** `INTEGRATIONS_API_KEY` 仅在 Edge Function 服务端读取，严禁暴露到前端。
- **错误处理：** 务必处理 429（配额超限）和 402（余额不足）。
- **计费：** 每次调用计费，折扣价 ¥0.13/次。
- **数值类型注意：** `open`/`close`/`high`/`low`/`volume` 为 string 类型，使用时需 `parseFloat()`；均线字段已是 number 类型。
- **period 说明：** 仅支持 1、5、15、30、60、120 分钟，如需日K及以上请使用 kline 接口。

AgentThinkAction(thought="Good. The API supports:\n- kline: period 101=日K, 102=周K, 103=月K\n- mink: 1/5/15/30/60/120 分钟K (for intraday)\n\nFor 分时图 (intraday), there's the mink API which gives minute-level data. The standard 分时图 in Chinese stock software shows price/volume over a trading day (9:30-15:00). The mink API returns minute K-line data with limited pageSize. For a full day's 分时图, we'd need 240 bars (4 hours * 60 minutes = 240 1-minute bars). \n\nSo the plan:\n1. Add period selector: 分时(1min) / 日K / 周K / 月K\n2. For 分时, use `stock-mink` edge function with period=1, pageSize=240\n3. For 日/周/月K, use `stock-kline` edge function with period=101/102/103, pageSize=120/52/60\n4. Time axis panning: implement a zoom/pan state with `startIndex` and `endIndex` to slice the data shown. Use left/right buttons or drag.\n\nFor time axis panning across all charts, I'll:\n- Maintain a `viewWindow: { start: number, end: number }` state\n- All charts slice `chartData.slice(start, end)` \n- Provide prev/next arrow buttons to shift the window\n\nFor 分时图, the layout changes significantly:\n- Show price line chart (not candlestick) \n- Show volume below\n- Show MACD/SKDJ still based on the minute data\n- No 四量图 (since 四量 algorithm is based on daily candles with volume comparisons)\n\nLet me now look at the existing Edge Functions and component structure to know what to keep/update.\n\nThe current edge function is `stock-kline`. ```
// 沪深分钟K线（含均线）Edge Function
import { serve } from "https://deno.land/std@0.168.0/http/server.ts";

const CORS = {
  "Access-Control-Allow-Origin": "*",
  "Access-Control-Allow-Headers": "authorization, x-client-info, apikey, content-type",
};

serve(async (req: Request): Promise<Response> => {
  if (req.method === "OPTIONS") return new Response("ok", { headers: CORS });
  if (req.method !== "POST") return new Response("Method Not Allowed", { status: 405 });

  let code: string, period: string, pageSize: string;
  try {
    const body = await req.json();
    code = body.code;
    if (!code) throw new Error("Missing code");
    period = body.period ?? "1";
    pageSize = body.pageSize ?? "240";
  } catch {
    return new Response(JSON.stringify({ error: "Invalid request body" }), {
      status: 400, headers: { ...CORS, "Content-Type": "application/json" },
    });
  }

  const apiKey = Deno.env.get("INTEGRATIONS_API_KEY");
  if (!apiKey) {
    return new Response(JSON.stringify({ error: "Server configuration error" }), {
      status: 500, headers: { ...CORS, "Content-Type": "application/json" },
    });
  }

  const upstream = await fetch(
    "https://app-csctj2dvhmo1-api-NLZ1o2xd6DE9-gateway.appmiaoda.com/stock/hs/mink",
    {
      method: "POST",
      headers: {
        "Content-Type": "application/x-www-form-urlencoded",
        "X-Gateway-Authorization": `Bearer ${apiKey}`,
      },
      body: new URLSearchParams({ code, period, pageSize }).toString(),
    }
  );

  if (upstream.status === 429 || upstream.status === 402) {
    return new Response(await upstream.text(), {
      status: upstream.status, headers: { ...CORS, "Content-Type": "application/json" },
    });
  }
  if (!upstream.ok) {
    return new Response(JSON.stringify({ error: `Upstream error: ${upstream.status}` }), {
      status: 502, headers: { ...CORS, "Content-Type": "application/json" },
    });
  }

  const data = await upstream.json();
  return new Response(JSON.stringify(data), {
    status: 200, headers: { ...CORS, "Content-Type": "application/json" },
  });
});

```

    50   const dea = calcEMA(dif, 9);
    51   const macd = dif.map((v, i) => (v - dea[i]) * 2);

    53 }
    54 function calcSKDJ(candles: Candle[], nPeriod = 9, mPeriod = 3) {
    55   const result: { K: number; D: number; J: number }[] = [];
    56   let prevK = 50, prevD = 50;
    57   for (let i = 0; i < candles.length; i++) {
    58     const start = Math.max(0, i - nPeriod + 1);
    59     const slice = candles.slice(start, i + 1);
    60     const lowest = Math.min(...slice.map((c) => c.low));
    61     const highest = Math.max(...slice.map((c) => c.high));
    62     const rsv = highest === lowest ? 50 : ((candles[i].close - lowest) / (highest - lowest)) * 100;
    63     const K = (prevK * (mPeriod - 1) + rsv) / mPeriod;
    64     const D = (prevD * (mPeriod - 1) + K) / mPeriod;
    65     const J = 3 * K - 2 * D;
    66     result.push({ K, D, J });
    67     prevK = K; prevD = D;
    68   }
    69   return result;
    70 }
    71 // ─── 四量图算法（通达信公式移植）──────────────────────────
    72 // 辅助：简单移动均线（不足期返回 null）
    73 function sma(data: number[], period: number): (number | null)[] {
    74   return data.map((_, i) => {
    75     if (i < period - 1) return null;
    76     return data.slice(i - period + 1, i + 1).reduce((a, b) => a + b, 0) / period;
    77   });
    78 }
    79 
    80 // 1. 散户量能：牛线/马线
    81 //    MID = (3*C + L + O + H) / 6
    82 //    牛线 = 加权MA(MID, 权重20..1，共20期) / 210
    83 //    马线 = MA(牛线, 6)
    84 //    红：C > 牛线；绿：C < 马线 || 牛线>=C>=马线 → 即 C <= 牛线（非红即绿简化）
    85 function calcSanhu(candles: Candle[]): (1 | -1)[] {
    86   const mids = candles.map(c => (3 * c.close + c.low + c.open + c.high) / 6);
    87   const bulls: (number | null)[] = mids.map((_, i) => {
    88     if (i < 20) return null;
    89     let sum = 0;
    90     for (let k = 0; k < 20; k++) sum += (20 - k) * mids[i - k];
    91     // REF(MID, 20) 用权重1
    92     sum += 1 * mids[i - 20];
    93     return sum / 210;
    94   });
    95   const bullArr = bulls.map(v => v ?? 0);
    96   const horses = sma(bullArr, 6);
    97   return candles.map((c, i) => {
    98     const bull = bulls[i];
    99     const horse = horses[i];
   100     if (bull == null || horse == null) return -1;
   101     if (c.close > bull) return 1;
   102     return -1; // C < 马线 or 中间都算绿（空仓/出逃）
   103   });
   104 }
   105 
   106 // 2. 游资量能：MAX/MIN(MA60, MA120)
   107 function calcYouzi(candles: Candle[]): (1 | -1)[] {
   108   const closes = candles.map(c => c.close);
   109   const ma60 = sma(closes, 60);
   110   const ma120 = sma(closes, 120);
   111   return candles.map((c, i) => {
   112     const a = ma60[i], b = ma120[i];
   113     if (a == null || b == null) return -1;
   114     const A = Math.max(a, b);
   115     return c.close >= A ? 1 : -1;
   116   });
   117 }
   118 
   119 // 3. 机构量能：MAX/MIN(MA45, MA90)
   120 function calcJigou(candles: Candle[]): (1 | -1)[] {
   121   const closes = candles.map(c => c.close);
   122   const ma45 = sma(closes, 45);
   123   const ma90 = sma(closes, 90);
   124   return candles.map((c, i) => {
   125     const a = ma45[i], b = ma90[i];
   126     if (a == null || b == null) return -1;
   127     const E = Math.max(a, b);
   128     return c.close > E ? 1 : -1;
   129   });
   130 }
   131 
   132 // 4. 主力量能：MAX/MIN(MA30, MA60)
   133 function calcZhuli(candles: Candle[]): (1 | -1)[] {
   134   const closes = candles.map(c => c.close);
   135   const ma30 = sma(closes, 30);
   136   const ma60 = sma(closes, 60);
   137   return candles.map((c, i) => {
   138     const a = ma30[i], b = ma60[i];
   139     if (a == null || b == null) return -1;
   140     const J = Math.max(a, b);
   141     return c.close > J ? 1 : -1;
   142   });
   143 }
   144 
   145 // 强弱钝化线：斐波那契MA [5,13,21,34,55,89,144,233]，score=sum-3.8
   146 const FIB_PERIODS = [5, 13, 21, 34, 55, 89, 144, 233];
   147 function calcQiangRuo(candles: Candle[]): (number | null)[] {
   148   const closes = candles.map(c => c.close);
   149   const fibMAs = FIB_PERIODS.map(p => sma(closes, p));
   150   return candles.map((c, i) => {
   151     // 只要最短MA有值才计算
   152     if (fibMAs[0][i] == null) return null;
   153     let score = 0;
   154     for (let k = 0; k < FIB_PERIODS.length; k++) {
   155       const ma = fibMAs[k][i];
   156       if (ma != null && c.close > ma) score++;
   157     }
   158     return +(score - 3.8).toFixed(2);
   159   });
   160 }
   161 
   162 interface LiangRow {
   163   date: string;
   164   val: 1;        // 柱高始终为1
   165   isRed: boolean;
   166   qiangRuo: number | null;
   167 }
   168 interface LiangData {
   169   sanhu: LiangRow[];
   170   youzi: LiangRow[];
   171   jigou: LiangRow[];
   172   zhuli: LiangRow[];
   173 }
   174 
   175 function calc4Liang(candles: Candle[]): LiangData {
   176   const sh = calcSanhu(candles);
   177   const yz = calcYouzi(candles);
   178   const jg = calcJigou(candles);
   179   const zl = calcZhuli(candles);
   180   const qr = calcQiangRuo(candles);
   181   return {
   182     sanhu: candles.map((c, i) => ({ date: c.date, val: 1, isRed: sh[i] === 1, qiangRuo: qr[i] })),
   183     youzi: candles.map((c, i) => ({ date: c.date, val: 1, isRed: yz[i] === 1, qiangRuo: qr[i] })),
   184     jigou: candles.map((c, i) => ({ date: c.date, val: 1, isRed: jg[i] === 1, qiangRuo: qr[i] })),
   185     zhuli: candles.map((c, i) => ({ date: c.date, val: 1, isRed: zl[i] === 1, qiangRuo: qr[i] })),
   186   };
   187 }
   188 
   189 // ─── 格式化 ──────────────────────────────────────────────
   190 function fmt(v: number | undefined, d = 2) {
   191   if (v == null || isNaN(v)) return '--';
   192   return v.toFixed(d);
   193 }
   194 function fmtWan(v: number | undefined) {
   195   if (v == null || isNaN(v)) return '--';
   196   if (v >= 1e8) return (v / 1e8).toFixed(2) + '亿';
   197   if (v >= 1e4) return (v / 1e4).toFixed(2) + '万';
   198   return v.toString();
   199 }

   209 // ─── 蜡烛图自定义Shape（堆叠Bar上层的实体+影线）──────────────
   210 // eslint-disable-next-line @typescript-eslint/no-explicit-any
   211 function CandleBody(props: any) {
   212   // props来自recharts Bar shape，包含 x, y, width, height, payload
   213   const { x, y, width, height, payload } = props;
   214   if (!payload || width <= 0) return null;
   215   const { open, close } = payload as Candle;
   216   const isUp = close >= open;
   217   const color = isUp ? RISE : FALL;
   218   const barWidth = Math.max(width - 2, 2);
   219   const barX = x + (width - barWidth) / 2;
   220   return (
   221     <rect x={barX} y={y} width={barWidth} height={Math.max(height, 1)} fill={color} />
   222   );
   223 }
   224 
   225 // 影线：从 high 到 low，细线居中
   226 // eslint-disable-next-line @typescript-eslint/no-explicit-any
   227 function CandleWick(props: any) {
   228   const { x, y, width, height, payload } = props;
   229   if (!payload || width <= 0) return null;
   230   const cx = x + width / 2;
   231   const isUp = (payload as Candle).close >= (payload as Candle).open;
   232   const color = isUp ? RISE : FALL;
   233   return (
   234     <line x1={cx} x2={cx} y1={y} y2={y + height} stroke={color} strokeWidth={1.5} />
   235   );
   236 }

   543 // ─── 图表行类型 ────────────────────────────────────────
   544 interface ChartRow extends Candle {
   545   isUp: boolean;
   546   s1: number; s2: number; s3: number; s4: number;
   547   ma5: number | null; ma10: number | null; ma20: number | null; ma30: number | null; ma60: number | null;
   548   vol5avg: number;
   549   dif: number | null; dea: number | null; macd: number | null;
   550   K: number | null; D: number | null; J: number | null;
   551 }
   552 
   553 // ─── 数据整合 ──────────────────────────────────────────
   554 function buildChartData(candles: Candle[]): ChartRow[] {
   555   const closes = candles.map(c => c.close);
   556   const macdCalc = closes.length >= 26 ? calcMACD(closes) : null;
   557   const skdjCalc = candles.length >= 9 ? calcSKDJ(candles) : null;
   558 
   559   const mas = MA_PERIODS.map(p => calcMA(closes, p));
   560   const vol5avg: number[] = candles.map((_, i) => {
   561     const start = Math.max(0, i - 4);
   562     return Math.round(candles.slice(start, i + 1).reduce((s, c) => s + c.volume, 0) / (i - start + 1));
   563   });
   564 
   565   const allLows = candles.map(c => c.low);
   566   const allHighs = candles.map(c => c.high);
   567   const minLow = Math.min(...allLows);
   568   const maxHigh = Math.max(...allHighs);
   569   const minBodySize = (maxHigh - minLow) * 0.002;
   570 
   571   return candles.map((c, i) => {
   572     const bodyLow = Math.min(c.open, c.close);
   573     const bodyHigh = Math.max(c.open, c.close);
   574     return {
   575       ...c,
   576       isUp: c.close >= c.open,
   577       s1: c.low,
   578       s2: bodyLow - c.low,
   579       s3: Math.max(bodyHigh - bodyLow, minBodySize),
   580       s4: c.high - bodyHigh,
   581       ma5: mas[0][i],
   582       ma10: mas[1][i],
   583       ma20: mas[2][i],
   584       ma30: mas[3][i],
   585       ma60: mas[4][i],
   586       vol5avg: vol5avg[i],
   587       dif: macdCalc ? +macdCalc.dif[i].toFixed(3) : null,
   588       dea: macdCalc ? +macdCalc.dea[i].toFixed(3) : null,
   589       macd: macdCalc ? +macdCalc.macd[i].toFixed(3) : null,
   590       K: skdjCalc ? +skdjCalc[i].K.toFixed(2) : null,
   591       D: skdjCalc ? +skdjCalc[i].D.toFixed(2) : null,
   592       J: skdjCalc ? +skdjCalc[i].J.toFixed(2) : null,
   593     } satisfies ChartRow;
   594   });
   595 }

// ─── 主组件 ──────────────────────────────────────────────
interface Props { stock: Stock; onClose: () => void; }

export default function StockDetailPanel({ stock, onClose }: Props) {
  const [info, setInfo] = useState<StockInfo | null>(null);
  const [candles, setCandles] = useState<Candle[]>([]);
  const [loading, setLoading] = useState(true);
  const [error, setError] = useState<string | null>(null);
  const abortRef = useRef<AbortController | null>(null);
  const isListed = stock.market !== '未上市' && !stock.code.includes('未上市');

  const load = useCallback(async () => {
    if (!isListed) { setLoading(false); return; }
    abortRef.current?.abort();
    abortRef.current = new AbortController();
    setLoading(true); setError(null);
    try {
      const [infoRes, klineRes] = await Promise.all([
        supabase.functions.invoke('stock-info', { body: { code: stock.code } }),
        supabase.functions.invoke('stock-kline', { body: { code: stock.code, period: '101', fuquan: '1', pageSize: '120' } }),
      ]);
      if (infoRes.error) throw infoRes.error;
      if (klineRes.error) throw klineRes.error;
      if (infoRes.data?.code === 200) setInfo(infoRes.data.data);
      if (klineRes.data?.code === 200) {
        const raw = klineRes.data.data;
        const parsed: Candle[] = (raw.candle as number[][]).map((row) => ({
          date: new Date(row[0] * 1000).toLocaleDateString('zh-CN', { month: '2-digit', day: '2-digit' }),
          open: row[1], close: row[2], high: row[3], low: row[4],
          volume: row[5], amount: row[6], change: row[7], changeRate: row[8],
        }));
        setCandles(parsed);
      }
    } catch (e: unknown) {
      if (e instanceof Error && e.name !== 'AbortError') setError(e.message);
    } finally { setLoading(false); }
  }, [stock.code, isListed]);

  useEffect(() => { load(); return () => abortRef.current?.abort(); }, [load]);

  const changeColor = info
    ? info.px_change_rate > 0 ? RISE : info.px_change_rate < 0 ? FALL : '#94a3b8'
    : '#94a3b8';

  const display60 = candles.slice(-60);
  const chartData = display60.length > 0 ? buildChartData(display60) : [];
  const liangData = display60.length > 0 ? calc4Liang(display60) : null;

  // K线图 Y轴 domain 需要0到maxP（堆叠从0起）
  const allPrices = display60.flatMap(c => [c.high, c.low]);
  const minLow = allPrices.length ? Math.min(...allPrices) * 0.999 : 0;
  const maxHigh = allPrices.length ? Math.max(...allPrices) * 1.001 : 0;
  const tickInterval = Math.floor(display60.length / 5);
```
New String: ```
// ─── 周期配置 ──────────────────────────────────────────
type PeriodKey = 'fens' | '101' | '102' | '103';
const PERIOD_CONFIG: Record<PeriodKey, { label: string; pageSize: string; isMink: boolean; dateFormat: (ts: number | string) => string }> = {
  fens: { label: '分时', pageSize: '240', isMink: true,
    dateFormat: (s: number | string) => {
      const str = String(s);
      return str.length >= 16 ? str.slice(11, 16) : str; // HH:mm
    }
  },
  '101': { label: '日K', pageSize: '120', isMink: false,
    dateFormat: (ts: number | string) => new Date(Number(ts) * 1000).toLocaleDateString('zh-CN', { month: '2-digit', day: '2-digit' }),
  },
  '102': { label: '周K', pageSize: '104', isMink: false,
    dateFormat: (ts: number | string) => new Date(Number(ts) * 1000).toLocaleDateString('zh-CN', { month: '2-digit', day: '2-digit' }),
  },
  '103': { label: '月K', pageSize: '60', isMink: false,
    dateFormat: (ts: number | string) => new Date(Number(ts) * 1000).toLocaleDateString('zh-CN', { year: '2-digit', month: '2-digit' }),
  },
};

// 分时图行数据
interface MinkRow {
  date: string; // HH:mm
  open: number; close: number; high: number; low: number;
  volume: number;
  ma5: number | null; ma10: number | null; ma30: number | null;
  preclose: number;
  changeRate: number;
}

const VIEW_SIZE = 60; // 每次显示的蜡烛数量

// ─── 主组件 ──────────────────────────────────────────────
interface Props { stock: Stock; onClose: () => void; }

export default function StockDetailPanel({ stock, onClose }: Props) {
  const [info, setInfo] = useState<StockInfo | null>(null);
  const [candles, setCandles] = useState<Candle[]>([]);
  const [minkRows, setMinkRows] = useState<MinkRow[]>([]);
  const [period, setPeriod] = useState<PeriodKey>('101');
  const [viewOffset, setViewOffset] = useState(0); // 0=最新，正=向历史移动
  const [loading, setLoading] = useState(true);
  const [error, setError] = useState<string | null>(null);
  const abortRef = useRef<AbortController | null>(null);
  const isListed = stock.market !== '未上市' && !stock.code.includes('未上市');

  const loadData = useCallback(async (p: PeriodKey) => {
    if (!isListed) { setLoading(false); return; }
    abortRef.current?.abort();
    abortRef.current = new AbortController();
    setLoading(true); setError(null); setViewOffset(0);
    const cfg = PERIOD_CONFIG[p];
    try {
      if (cfg.isMink) {
        // 分时图：只需 mink + info
        const [infoRes, minkRes] = await Promise.all([
          supabase.functions.invoke('stock-info', { body: { code: stock.code } }),
          supabase.functions.invoke('stock-mink', { body: { code: stock.code, period: '1', pageSize: cfg.pageSize } }),
        ]);
        if (infoRes.error) throw infoRes.error;
        if (minkRes.error) throw minkRes.error;
        if (infoRes.data?.code === 200) setInfo(infoRes.data.data);
        if (minkRes.data?.code === 200) {
          const list = minkRes.data.data.list as {
            day: string; open: string; close: string; high: string; low: string;
            volume: string; ma_price5: number; ma_price10: number; ma_price30: number;
          }[];
          const preclose = infoRes.data?.data?.preclose_px ?? parseFloat(list[0]?.open ?? '0');
          const rows: MinkRow[] = list.map(item => {
            const close = parseFloat(item.close);
            return {
              date: cfg.dateFormat(item.day),
              open: parseFloat(item.open), close,
              high: parseFloat(item.high), low: parseFloat(item.low),
              volume: parseFloat(item.volume),
              ma5: item.ma_price5 ?? null,
              ma10: item.ma_price10 ?? null,
              ma30: item.ma_price30 ?? null,
              preclose,
              changeRate: preclose > 0 ? +((close - preclose) / preclose * 100).toFixed(2) : 0,
            };
          });
          setMinkRows(rows);
          setCandles([]);
        }
      } else {
        // K线
        const [infoRes, klineRes] = await Promise.all([
          supabase.functions.invoke('stock-info', { body: { code: stock.code } }),
          supabase.functions.invoke('stock-kline', { body: { code: stock.code, period: p, fuquan: '1', pageSize: cfg.pageSize } }),
        ]);
        if (infoRes.error) throw infoRes.error;
        if (klineRes.error) throw klineRes.error;
        if (infoRes.data?.code === 200) setInfo(infoRes.data.data);
        if (klineRes.data?.code === 200) {
          const raw = klineRes.data.data;
          const parsed: Candle[] = (raw.candle as number[][]).map((row) => ({
            date: cfg.dateFormat(row[0]),
            open: row[1], close: row[2], high: row[3], low: row[4],
            volume: row[5], amount: row[6], change: row[7], changeRate: row[8],
          }));
          setCandles(parsed);
          setMinkRows([]);
        }
      }
    } catch (e: unknown) {
      if (e instanceof Error && e.name !== 'AbortError') setError(e.message);
    } finally { setLoading(false); }
  }, [stock.code, isListed]);

  useEffect(() => { loadData(period); return () => abortRef.current?.abort(); }, [loadData, period]);

  const handlePeriodChange = (p: PeriodKey) => { setPeriod(p); };

  const changeColor = info
    ? info.px_change_rate > 0 ? RISE : info.px_change_rate < 0 ? FALL : '#94a3b8'
    : '#94a3b8';

  // 分时数据视图（不做pan，直接用全量）
  const isFens = period === 'fens';

  // 时间轴平移逻辑（仅对K线）
  const totalBars = candles.length;
  const maxOffset = Math.max(0, totalBars - VIEW_SIZE);
  const safeOffset = Math.min(viewOffset, maxOffset);
  const viewEnd = totalBars - safeOffset;
  const viewStart = Math.max(0, viewEnd - VIEW_SIZE);
  const displayCandles = candles.slice(viewStart, viewEnd);

  const chartData = displayCandles.length > 0 ? buildChartData(displayCandles) : [];
  const liangData = displayCandles.length > 0 ? calc4Liang(displayCandles) : null;

  const allPrices = displayCandles.flatMap(c => [c.high, c.low]);
  const minLow = allPrices.length ? Math.min(...allPrices) * 0.999 : 0;
  const maxHigh = allPrices.length ? Math.max(...allPrices) * 1.001 : 0;
  const tickInterval = Math.floor((isFens ? minkRows.length : displayCandles.length) / 5);

  // 分时图Y轴范围
  const minkPrices = minkRows.flatMap(r => [r.high, r.low]).filter(Boolean);
  const minkMinY = minkPrices.length ? Math.min(...minkPrices) * 0.999 : 0;
  const minkMaxY = minkPrices.length ? Math.max(...minkPrices) * 1.001 : 0;

  const canPanLeft = safeOffset < maxOffset;
  const canPanRight = safeOffset > 0;
```

              </div>
            )}
